\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename Scalar\+\_\+, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{classEigen_1_1TensorFixedSize_ad59d5f115a7ebf5f55f184ca09ab1609}{Dimensions}}, int Options\+\_\+ = 0, typename Index\+Type = Dense\+Index$>$\newline
class Eigen\+::\+Tensor\+Fixed\+Size$<$ Scalar\+\_\+, Dimensions, Options\+\_\+, Index\+Type $>$}
The fixed sized version of the tensor class. 

The fixed sized equivalent of Eigen\+::\+Tensor$<$float, 3$>$ t(3, 5, 7); is Eigen\+::\+Tensor\+Fixed\+Size$<$float, Sizes$<$3,5,7$>$$>$ t;
